Mr. Chairman, this amendment would repeal H.R. 50 if GDP remains below 5 percent over the first four quarters after enactment. H.R. 50 is not intended to eliminate the deficit in the first year. It is simply a limitation on the growth rate of GDP over that period of time in order to get at the deficit in the long term.  The question here is not whether to leave the tax provisions in place or not to repeal the State and local income tax provisions. They have been removed so that we have less spending than we would if those provisions remain in place. I urge support of the amendment.   238 ACTING PRESIDENT pro tempore.
